8. Forecasting Roadmap

  • Holt-Winters: Recursive α=0.3/β=0.1 over 78-obs 3x-weighted series. Bi-weekly cadence enforcement applied post-forecast for steady items.
  • Croston's: α=0.3, demand/interval refined 70% L13W / 30% smoothed. Event calendar insertions applied at Prime Day and Fall Deal windows.
  • Heuristic: Ramp weeks 1-6 post-launch excluded. Post-ramp avg → L13W → L52W fallback chain.
  • Inactive: Zero forecast. Alert written if prior projection > 0.
  • Alert threshold: 5% variance vs manual projections.
  • Risk flags: 3052 records with sparse history | 1871 outlier weeks detected | 1453 non-stationary series.
